<h2><span id=".E4.BA.BA.E9.A1.9E.E5.88.A9.E7.94.A8"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="人類利用">人類利用</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%9C%9F%E8%8F%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="编辑章节：人類利用">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:S_cerevisiae_under_DIC_microscopy.jpg"><img alt="Microscopic view of five spherical structures; one of the spheres is considerably smaller than the rest and attached to one of the larger spheres" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1560" data-file-width="1560" decoding="async" height="170" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d9/S_cerevisiae_under_DIC_microscopy.jpg/170px-S_cerevisiae_under_DIC_microscopy.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d9/S_cerevisiae_under_DIC_microscopy.jpg/255px-S_cerevisiae_under_DIC_microscopy.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d9/S_cerevisiae_under_DIC_microscopy.jpg/340px-S_cerevisiae_under_DIC_microscopy.jpg 2x" width="170"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:S_cerevisiae_under_DIC_microscopy.jpg" title="放大"></a></div><a href="/wiki/%E5%BE%AE%E5%88%86%E5%B9%B2%E6%B6%89%E7%9B%B8%E5%B7%AE%E6%98%BE%E5%BE%AE%E9%95%9C" title="微分干涉相差显微镜">微分干涉相差顯微鏡</a>視野下的<a href="/wiki/%E9%87%80%E9%85%92%E9%85%B5%E6%AF%8D" title="釀酒酵母">釀酒酵母</a></div></div></div>
<p><span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Ethnomycology" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="人類真菌學"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%BA%BA%E9%A1%9E%E7%9C%9F%E8%8F%8C%E5%AD%B8&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="人類真菌學（页面不存在）">人類真菌學</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ethnomycology" title="en:Ethnomycology"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Ethnomycology</span></a></span>）</span></span>是研究人類利用真菌的歷史，以及真菌對人類社會影響的學門。長久以來，人類利用真菌來製造、保存食物，或用作其他用途。在許多國家<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Fungiculture" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="蕈類養殖"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%95%88%E9%A1%9E%E9%A4%8A%E6%AE%96&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="蕈類養殖（页面不存在）">蕈類養殖</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fungiculture" title="en:Fungiculture"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Fungiculture</span></a></span>）</span></span>與<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Mushroom hunting" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="蕈類採集"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%95%88%E9%A1%9E%E6%8E%A1%E9%9B%86&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="蕈類採集（页面不存在）">蕈類採集</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mushroom_hunting" title="en:Mushroom hunting"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Mushroom hunting</span></a></span>）</span></span>都是重要產業。因為許多真菌可以生產有生物活性的<a href="/wiki/%E5%A4%A9%E7%84%B6%E4%BA%A7%E7%89%A9" title="天然产物">天然產物</a>與抗生素，許多真菌已被開發、或正被開發以大量生產抗生素、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%B6%AD%E4%BB%96%E5%91%BD" title="維他命">維他命</a>、抗癌藥物或降低<a href="/wiki/%E8%86%BD%E5%9B%BA%E9%86%87" title="膽固醇">膽固醇</a>的藥物。近期隨著在真菌進行<a href="/wiki/%E5%9F%BA%E5%9B%A0%E5%B7%A5%E7%A8%8B" title="基因工程">基因工程</a>的技術發展，使真菌的<a href="/wiki/%E4%BB%A3%E8%AC%9D%E5%B7%A5%E7%A8%8B%E5%AD%B8" title="代謝工程學">代謝工程</a>應用成為可能<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Finsham1989_205-0"><a href="#cite_note-Finsham1989-205">[199]</a></sup>。例如基因修飾後的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%85%B5%E6%AF%8D%E8%8F%8C" title="酵母菌">酵母菌</a>可以用來大量生產許多藥物<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Hawkins2008_206-0"><a href="#cite_note-Hawkins2008-206">[200]</a></sup>，且因為酵母菌在培養箱中生長迅速，使生產藥物的效率比從原本的來源提煉還要高<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Huang2008_207-0"><a href="#cite_note-Huang2008-207">[201]</a></sup>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E8.97.A5.E7.94.A8"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="藥用">藥用</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%9C%9F%E8%8F%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="编辑章节：藥用">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span id=".E7.95.B6.E4.BB.A3.E8.97.A5.E7.94.A8"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="當代藥用">當代藥用</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%9C%9F%E8%8F%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;section=35" title="编辑章节：當代藥用">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%97%A5%E7%94%A8%E7%9C%9F%E8%8F%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="藥用真菌（页面不存在）">藥用真菌</a></div>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Penicillium_notatum.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="615" data-file-width="640" decoding="async" height="211" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Penicillium_notatum.jpg/220px-Penicillium_notatum.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Penicillium_notatum.jpg/330px-Penicillium_notatum.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Penicillium_notatum.jpg/440px-Penicillium_notatum.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Penicillium_notatum.jpg" title="放大"></a></div><a href="/wiki/%E4%BA%A7%E9%BB%84%E9%9D%92%E9%9C%89%E8%8F%8C" title="产黄青霉菌">產黃青黴菌</a>可以合成<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%8B%84%E9%9D%92%E9%BB%B4%E7%B4%A0" title="苄青黴素">苄青黴素</a></div></div></div>
<p><br/>
許多真菌產生的代謝物可以作為藥物。最著名的例子便是包括<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%9D%92%E9%BB%B4%E7%B4%A0" title="青黴素">青黴素</a>在內的<a href="/wiki/%E6%8A%97%E7%94%9F%E7%B4%A0" title="抗生素">抗生素</a>。在自然界中，真菌或細菌產生的抗生素通常有兩種功用，一是高濃度時作為抑制其他微生物生長的抑制劑，以避免其他微生物與自己競爭資源，二是低濃度時作為物種內或物種間<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%BE%A4%E9%AB%94%E6%84%9F%E6%87%89" title="群體感應">群體感應</a>的訊息傳遞分子<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Fajardo2008_208-0"><a href="#cite_note-Fajardo2008-208">[202]</a></sup> 。自然界中產生的青黴素<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%8B%84%E9%9D%92%E9%BB%B4%E7%B4%A0" title="苄青黴素">苄青黴素</a>（由<a href="/wiki/%E4%BA%A7%E9%BB%84%E9%9D%92%E9%9C%89%E8%8F%8C" title="产黄青霉菌">產黃青黴菌</a>產生）可以有效殺死的細菌相對有限，但其他各式種類的青黴素可用<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%8C%96%E5%AD%B8%E5%90%88%E6%88%90" title="化學合成">化學方法</a>合成，以達到更廣泛的殺菌能力，現代使用的青黴素便是<a href="/wiki/%E5%8D%8A%E5%90%88%E6%88%90" title="半合成">半合成</a>的產物，先由真菌合成，再針對需要的特殊性質對其進行化學修飾而得到最終產物<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Brakhage2004_209-0"><a href="#cite_note-Brakhage2004-209">[203]</a></sup>。除了青黴素外，由真菌生產的抗生素還包括<a href="/wiki/%E7%8E%AF%E5%AD%A2%E7%B4%A0" title="环孢素">環孢素</a>（在<a href="/wiki/%E5%99%A8%E5%AE%98%E7%A7%BB%E6%A4%8D" title="器官移植">器官移植</a>時用作<a href="/wiki/%E5%85%8D%E7%96%AB%E6%8A%91%E5%88%B6%E5%8A%91" title="免疫抑制劑">免疫抑制劑</a>）、<a href="/wiki/%E5%A4%AB%E8%A5%BF%E5%9C%B0%E9%85%B8" title="夫西地酸">夫西地酸</a>（可用來處理<a href="/wiki/%E8%80%90%E7%94%B2%E6%B0%A7%E8%A5%BF%E6%9E%97%E9%87%91%E9%BB%84%E8%89%B2%E8%91%A1%E8%90%84%E7%90%83%E8%8F%8C" title="耐甲氧西林金黄色葡萄球菌">耐甲氧西林金黄色葡萄球菌</a>的感染<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Pan2008_210-0"><a href="#cite_note-Pan2008-210">[204]</a></sup> ）與<a href="/wiki/%E7%81%B0%E9%BB%83%E9%BB%B4%E7%B4%A0" title="灰黃黴素">灰黃黴素</a>（可治療<a href="/wiki/%E7%9C%9F%E8%8F%8C%E7%97%85" title="真菌病">真菌感染</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Loo2006_211-0"><a href="#cite_note-Loo2006-211">[205]</a></sup>）。
另外，可以抑制<a href="/wiki/%E7%BE%9F%E7%94%B2%E5%9F%BA%E6%88%8A%E4%BA%8C%E9%85%B8%E5%8D%95%E9%85%B0%E8%BE%85%E9%85%B6A%E8%BF%98%E5%8E%9F%E9%85%B6" title="羟甲基戊二酸单酰辅酶A还原酶">羥甲基戊二酸單醯輔酶A還原酶</a>，繼而抑制<a href="/wiki/%E8%86%BD%E5%9B%BA%E9%86%87" title="膽固醇">膽固醇</a>合成的<a href="/wiki/%E4%BB%96%E6%B1%80" title="他汀">他汀</a>類藥物，許多也是由真菌合成的，例如由<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Penicillium citrinum" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="橘青黴"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%A9%98%E9%9D%92%E9%BB%B4&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="橘青黴（页面不存在）">橘青黴</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Penicillium_citrinum" title="en:Penicillium citrinum"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Penicillium citrinum</span></a></span>）</span></span>合成的<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Mevastatin" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="美伐他汀"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%BE%8E%E4%BC%90%E4%BB%96%E6%B1%80&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="美伐他汀（页面不存在）">美伐他汀</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mevastatin" title="en:Mevastatin"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Mevastatin</span></a></span>）</span></span>，以及由<a href="/wiki/%E5%9C%9F%E9%BA%B4%E9%BB%B4" title="土麴黴">土麴黴</a>與<a href="/wiki/%E5%B9%B3%E8%8F%87" title="平菇">平菇</a>合成的<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Lovastatin" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="洛伐他汀"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%B4%9B%E4%BC%90%E4%BB%96%E6%B1%80&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="洛伐他汀（页面不存在）">洛伐他汀</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lovastatin" title="en:Lovastatin"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Lovastatin</span></a></span>）</span></span><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Manzoni2002_212-0"><a href="#cite_note-Manzoni2002-212">[206]</a></sup>。真菌也能生產抑制<a href="/wiki/%E7%97%85%E6%AF%92" title="病毒">病毒</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-elMekkawy1998_213-0"><a href="#cite_note-elMekkawy1998-213">[207]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ElDine2008_214-0"><a href="#cite_note-ElDine2008-214">[208]</a></sup>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%99%8C%E7%B4%B0%E8%83%9E" title="癌細胞">癌細胞</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Hetland2008_215-0"><a href="#cite_note-Hetland2008-215">[209]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Yuen2005_216-0"><a href="#cite_note-Yuen2005-216">[210]</a></sup>生長的藥物，例如產於<a href="/wiki/%E9%9B%B2%E8%8A%9D" title="雲芝">雲芝</a>的抗癌藥物<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Polysaccharide-K" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="雲芝多醣K"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9B%B2%E8%8A%9D%E5%A4%9A%E9%86%A3K&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="雲芝多醣K（页面不存在）">雲芝多醣K</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polysaccharide-K" title="en:Polysaccharide-K"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Polysaccharide-K</span></a></span>）</span></span>已在歐洲與日本等地作為抗癌藥物的<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Adjuvant" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="佐劑"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%BD%90%E5%8A%91&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="佐劑（页面不存在）">佐劑</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Adjuvant" title="en:Adjuvant"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Adjuvant</span></a></span>）</span></span>使用<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Fisher2002_217-0"><a href="#cite_note-Fisher2002-217">[211]</a></sup>，產於<a href="/wiki/%E9%A6%99%E8%8F%87" title="香菇">香菇</a>的<a href="/wiki/%E9%A6%99%E8%8F%87%E5%A4%9A%E7%B3%96" title="香菇多糖">香菇多糖</a>也在日本等國被用在癌症治療中<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Sullivan2006_218-0"><a href="#cite_note-Sullivan2006-218">[212]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Halpern2002_219-0"><a href="#cite_note-Halpern2002-219">[213]</a></sup>。
</p>
<h4><span id=".E5.82.B3.E7.B5.B1.E9.86.AB.E5.AD.B8"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="傳統醫學">傳統醫學</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%9C%9F%E8%8F%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="编辑章节：傳統醫學">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r70089473/mw-parser-output/.tmulti">.mw-parser-output .tmulti .thumbinner{display:flex;flex-direction:column}.mw-parser-output .tmulti .theader{clear:both;font-weight:bold;text-align:center;align-self:center;background-color:transparent;width:100%}.mw-parser-output .tmulti .thumbcaption{background-color:transparent}.mw-parser-output .trow{justify-content:center}.mw-parser-output .tmulti .tsingle{float:none!important;max-width:100%!important;box-sizing:border-box;text-align:center}.mw-parser-output .tmulti .tsingle .thumbcaption{text-align:left}.mw-parser-output .tmulti .trow>.thumbcaption{text-align:center}}</style><div class="thumb tmulti tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:328px;max-width:328px"><div class="trow"><div class="tsingle" style="width:142px;max-width:142px"><div class="thumbimage"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Ganoderma_lucidum_01.jpg"><img alt="Upper surface view of a kidney-shaped fungus, brownish-red with a lighter yellow-brown margin, and a somewhat varnished or shiny appearance" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="800" decoding="async" height="105" //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/81/Ganoderma_lucidum_01.jpg/280px-Ganoderma_lucidum_01.jpg 2x" width="140"/></a></div></div><div class="tsingle" style="width:182px;max-width:182px"><div class="thumbimage"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:CordycepsSinensis.jpg"><img alt="Two dried yellow-orange caterpillars, one with a curly grayish fungus growing out of one of its ends. The grayish fungus is roughly equal to or slightly greater in length than the caterpillar, and tapers in thickness to a narrow end." data-file-height="1136" data-file-width="1948" decoding="async" height="105" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/94/CordycepsSinensis.jpg/180px-CordycepsSinensis.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/94/CordycepsSinensis.jpg/270px-CordycepsSinensis.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/94/CordycepsSinensis.jpg/360px-CordycepsSinensis.jpg 2x" width="180"/></a></div></div></div><div class="trow" style="display:flex"><div class="thumbcaption">兩種中醫常用的藥用真菌：<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%B5%A4%E8%8A%9D&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="赤芝（页面不存在）">赤芝</a>（左）與<a href="/wiki/%E5%86%AC%E8%99%AB%E5%A4%8F%E8%8D%89" title="冬虫夏草">冬虫夏草</a>（右）</div></div></div></div>
<p>許多真菌是<a href="/wiki/%E4%B8%AD%E5%8C%BB%E5%AD%A6" title="中医学">中醫</a>等<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%82%B3%E7%B5%B1%E9%86%AB%E5%AD%B8" title="傳統醫學">傳統醫學</a>使用的藥材，中醫用來入藥的真菌包括<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%A7%AC%E6%9D%BE%E8%8C%B8" title="姬松茸">姬松茸</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Hetland2008_215-1"><a href="#cite_note-Hetland2008-215">[209]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Firenzuoli2008_220-0"><a href="#cite_note-Firenzuoli2008-220">[214]</a></sup>、<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%B5%A4%E8%8A%9D&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="赤芝（页面不存在）">赤芝</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Paterson2006_221-0"><a href="#cite_note-Paterson2006-221">[215]</a></sup>與<a href="/wiki/%E5%86%AC%E8%99%AB%E5%A4%8F%E8%8D%89" title="冬虫夏草">冬蟲夏草</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Paterson2008_222-0"><a href="#cite_note-Paterson2008-222">[216]</a></sup>等。冬蟲夏草是<a href="/wiki/%E5%AD%90%E5%9B%8A%E8%8F%8C%E9%97%A8" title="子囊菌门">子囊菌門</a>的真菌中華蟲草寄生於<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Hepialidae" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="蝙蝠蛾"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%9D%99%E8%9D%A0%E8%9B%BE&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="蝙蝠蛾（页面不存在）">蝙蝠蛾</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hepialidae" title="en:Hepialidae"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Hepialidae</span></a></span>）</span></span>幼蟲後，死亡的幼蟲與菌絲所組成。最早將冬蟲夏草入藥的地方是<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%A5%BF%E8%97%8F" title="西藏">西藏</a>與<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%B0%BC%E6%B3%8A%E7%88%BE" title="尼泊爾">尼泊爾</a>，十五世紀的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%97%8F%E9%86%AB" title="藏醫">藏醫</a>醫生舒卡·年姆多吉（Zurkhar Nyamnyi Dorje）在其著作《藥方匯集》中提到冬蟲夏草，是冬蟲夏草用於傳統醫學的最早文字紀錄<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Winkler2008b_223-0"><a href="#cite_note-Winkler2008b-223">[217]</a></sup>。中國對冬蟲夏草最早的記載是<a href="/wiki/%E6%B8%85%E6%9C%9D" title="清朝">清朝</a><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%B1%AA%E6%98%82&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="汪昂（页面不存在）">汪昂</a>在《本草备要》一書中所寫「冬虫夏草，甘平，保肺益肾，止血化痰，止劳咳。四川嘉定府所产者佳。冬在土中，形如老蚕，有毛能动，至夏则毛出土上，连身俱化为草。若不取，至冬复化为虫。」<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Winkler2008_224-0"><a href="#cite_note-Winkler2008-224">[218]</a></sup>中醫認為冬蟲夏草是名貴滋補的草藥，有「甘平保肺，益腎止血，化痰，已勞嗽」之效<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-225"><a href="#cite_note-225">[219]</a></sup>。
</p><p>屬於<a href="/wiki/%E6%8B%85%E5%AD%90%E8%8F%8C%E9%97%A8" title="担子菌门">擔子菌門</a>的<a href="/wiki/%E6%A1%91%E9%BB%83" title="桑黃">桑黃</a>是另一種傳統醫學使用的草藥，<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%B8%AD%E9%86%AB" title="中醫">中醫</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%9F%93%E9%86%AB" title="韓醫">韓醫</a>與<a href="/wiki/%E6%97%A5%E6%9C%AC%E6%BC%A2%E6%96%B9%E9%86%AB%E5%AD%B8" title="日本漢方醫學">日本漢方醫學</a>皆有使用紀錄。早在秦漢時的《<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%A5%9E%E8%BE%B2%E6%9C%AC%E8%8D%89%E7%B6%93" title="神農本草經">神農本草經</a>》就有桑黃入藥的紀錄，中醫認為桑黃有止血與治療婦女病的功效，<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%9C%9D%E9%B2%9C%E6%97%B6%E4%BB%A3" title="朝鲜时代">朝鮮時代</a>的醫書《<a href="/wiki/%E4%B9%A1%E8%8D%AF%E9%9B%86%E6%88%90%E6%96%B9" title="乡药集成方">鄉藥集成方</a>》與《<a href="/wiki/%E6%9D%B1%E9%86%AB%E5%AF%B6%E9%91%91" title="東醫寶鑑">東醫寶鑑</a>》均記載桑黃有如靈丹妙藥，<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%B1%9F%E6%88%B6%E6%99%82%E4%BB%A3" title="江戶時代">江戶時代</a>的<a href="/wiki/%E6%97%A5%E6%9C%AC" title="日本">日本</a>也將桑黃當作漢方藥<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-226"><a href="#cite_note-226">[220]</a></sup>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E9.A3.9F.E7.94.A8"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="食用">食用</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%9C%9F%E8%8F%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;section=37" title="编辑章节：食用">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Asian_mushrooms.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="564" data-file-width="1024" decoding="async" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f8/Asian_mushrooms.jpg/300px-Asian_mushrooms.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f8/Asian_mushrooms.jpg/450px-Asian_mushrooms.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f8/Asian_mushrooms.jpg/600px-Asian_mushrooms.jpg 2x" width="300"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Asian_mushrooms.jpg" title="放大"></a></div>一些亞洲常見的<a href="/wiki/%E9%A3%9F%E7%94%A8%E8%95%88" title="食用蕈">食用蕈</a></div></div></div>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a href="/wiki/%E9%A3%9F%E7%94%A8%E8%95%88" title="食用蕈">食用蕈</a></div>
<p><a href="/wiki/%E9%A3%9F%E7%94%A8%E8%95%88" title="食用蕈">食用蕈</a>有些是野外採集的，有些則是商業種植的。西方最常食用的蕈類是<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%B4%8B%E8%8F%87" title="洋菇">洋菇</a>，用在沙拉、湯品與許多其他料理中。許多在亞洲常被種植、食用的蕈類，例如<a href="/wiki/%E8%8D%89%E8%8F%87" title="草菇">草菇</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E5%B9%B3%E8%8F%87" title="平菇">平菇</a>與<a href="/wiki/%E9%87%91%E9%87%9D%E8%8F%87" title="金針菇">金針菇</a>也漸漸傳到西方<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Stamets2000_227-0"><a href="#cite_note-Stamets2000-227">[221]</a></sup>。許多其他種蕈類可由野外採集來食用或販賣，包括<a href="/wiki/%E6%9D%BE%E4%B9%B3%E8%8F%87" title="松乳菇">松乳菇</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%BE%8A%E8%82%9A%E8%8F%8C" title="羊肚菌">羊肚菌</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E9%B8%A1%E6%B2%B9%E8%8F%87" title="鸡油菇">雞油菇</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E6%9D%BE%E9%9C%B2" title="松露">松露</a>、<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Craterellus" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="喇叭菌"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%96%87%E5%8F%AD%E8%8F%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="喇叭菌（页面不存在）">喇叭菌</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Craterellus" title="en:Craterellus"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Craterellus</span></a></span>）</span></span>與<a href="/wiki/%E7%BE%8E%E5%91%B3%E7%89%9B%E8%82%9D%E8%8F%8C" title="美味牛肝菌">美味牛肝菌</a>等，有些種類在市場上的價格十分高昂，通常是特殊料理中的食材<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-228"><a href="#cite_note-228">[222]</a></sup>。
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Blue_Stilton_Quarter_Front.jpg"><img alt="A corner of cheese with greenish streaks through it" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="700" data-file-width="903" decoding="async" height="171" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d3/Blue_Stilton_Quarter_Front.jpg/220px-Blue_Stilton_Quarter_Front.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d3/Blue_Stilton_Quarter_Front.jpg/330px-Blue_Stilton_Quarter_Front.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d3/Blue_Stilton_Quarter_Front.jpg/440px-Blue_Stilton_Quarter_Front.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Blue_Stilton_Quarter_Front.jpg" title="放大"></a></div><span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Penicillium roqueforti" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="羅克福青黴菌"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%BE%85%E5%85%8B%E7%A6%8F%E9%9D%92%E9%BB%B4%E8%8F%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="羅克福青黴菌（页面不存在）">羅克福青黴菌</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Penicillium_roqueforti" title="en:Penicillium roqueforti"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Penicillium roqueforti</span></a></span>）</span></span>產生<a href="/wiki/%E6%96%AF%E8%92%82%E7%88%BE%E9%A0%93%E8%8A%9D%E5%A3%AB" title="斯蒂爾頓芝士">斯蒂爾頓芝士</a>上的藍綠色花紋</div></div></div>
<p>生產某些種<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%B5%B7%E5%8F%B8" title="起司">起司</a>時需要把特定真菌加到<a href="/wiki/%E5%87%9D%E4%B9%B3" title="凝乳">凝乳</a>中，以產生特殊的風味或口感，例如<a href="/wiki/%E6%96%AF%E8%92%82%E7%88%BE%E9%A0%93%E8%8A%9D%E5%A3%AB" title="斯蒂爾頓芝士">斯蒂爾頓芝士</a>與<a href="/wiki/%E7%BD%97%E5%85%8B%E7%A6%8F%E5%B9%B2%E9%85%AA" title="罗克福干酪">羅克福乾酪</a>上的藍色紋路便是<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Penicillium roqueforti" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="羅克福青黴菌"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%BE%85%E5%85%8B%E7%A6%8F%E9%9D%92%E9%BB%B4%E8%8F%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="羅克福青黴菌（页面不存在）">羅克福青黴菌</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Penicillium_roqueforti" title="en:Penicillium roqueforti"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Penicillium roqueforti</span></a></span>）</span></span>造成的<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Kinsella1976_229-0"><a href="#cite_note-Kinsella1976-229">[223]</a></sup>。用於製造起司的真菌都是無毒的，但起司成熟或貯藏時，可能有其他種類的真菌生長於其上，而產生多種<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="mycotoxin" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="真菌毒素"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%9C%9F%E8%8F%8C%E6%AF%92%E7%B4%A0&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="真菌毒素（页面不存在）">真菌毒素</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/mycotoxin" title="en:mycotoxin"><span dir="auto" lang="en">mycotoxin</span></a></span>）</span></span>，是生產起司時需考慮的因素<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Erdogan2004_230-0"><a href="#cite_note-Erdogan2004-230">[224]</a></sup>。
</p>
<h4><span id=".E7.99.BC.E9.85.B5.E9.A3.9F.E5.93.81"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="發酵食品">發酵食品</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%9C%9F%E8%8F%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;section=38" title="编辑章节：發酵食品">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><a href="/wiki/%E9%87%80%E9%85%92%E9%85%B5%E6%AF%8D" title="釀酒酵母">釀酒酵母</a>常用來製作<a href="/wiki/%E9%BA%B5%E5%8C%85" title="麵包">麵包</a>與其他小麥加工食品<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Kulp2000_231-0"><a href="#cite_note-Kulp2000-231">[225]</a></sup>，許多酵母菌可用來<a href="/wiki/%E9%85%BF%E9%85%92" title="酿酒">釀酒</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Piskur2006_232-0"><a href="#cite_note-Piskur2006-232">[226]</a></sup>，<a href="/wiki/%E7%B1%B3%E9%BA%B4%E8%8F%8C" title="米麴菌">米麴菌</a>則可用來發酵大豆，製作<a href="/wiki/%E9%85%B1%E6%B2%B9" title="酱油">醬油</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E6%97%A5%E6%9C%AC%E9%85%92" title="日本酒">日本酒</a>與<a href="/wiki/%E5%91%B3%E5%99%8C" title="味噌">味噌</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Abe2006_233-0"><a href="#cite_note-Abe2006-233">[227]</a></sup>，<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%A0%B9%E9%9C%89" title="根霉">根黴</a>則是製作印尼食品<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%B8%B9%E8%B2%9D" title="丹貝">丹貝</a>的重要原料<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Hachmeister1993_234-0"><a href="#cite_note-Hachmeister1993-234">[228]</a></sup>。許多與這些真菌親緣相當接近的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%BA%B4%E8%8F%8C%E5%B1%AC" title="麴菌屬">麴菌屬</a>真菌會產生對人體有害的毒素，但這些真菌大多是<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%A6%B4%E5%8C%96" title="馴化">馴化物種</a>，經由育種、人擇選出發酵能力佳，又不會產生<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="mycotoxin" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="真菌毒素"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%9C%9F%E8%8F%8C%E6%AF%92%E7%B4%A0&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="真菌毒素（页面不存在）">真菌毒素</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/mycotoxin" title="en:mycotoxin"><span dir="auto" lang="en">mycotoxin</span></a></span>）</span></span>的真菌種類用於食品工業中<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Jorgensen2007_235-0"><a href="#cite_note-Jorgensen2007-235">[229]</a></sup> 。另外<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Quorn" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="闊恩牌素肉"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%97%8A%E6%81%A9%E7%89%8C%E7%B4%A0%E8%82%89&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="闊恩牌素肉（页面不存在）">闊恩牌素肉</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Quorn" title="en:Quorn"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Quorn</span></a></span>）</span></span>也是真菌衍生的食品，由<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Fusarium venenatum" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="金黃色鐮孢"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%87%91%E9%BB%83%E8%89%B2%E9%90%AE%E5%AD%A2&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="金黃色鐮孢（页面不存在）">金黃色鐮孢</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fusarium_venenatum" title="en:Fusarium venenatum"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Fusarium venenatum</span></a></span>）</span></span>發酵而成<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ODonnell1998_236-0"><a href="#cite_note-ODonnell1998-236">[230]</a></sup>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E6.9C.89.E6.AF.92.E7.9C.9F.E8.8F.8C"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="有毒真菌">有毒真菌</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%9C%9F%E8%8F%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;section=39" title="编辑章节：有毒真菌">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Amanita_phalloides_1.JPG"><img alt="Two light yellow-green mushrooms with stems and caps, one smaller and still in the ground, the larger one pulled out and laid beside the other to show its bulbous stem with a ring" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1600" data-file-width="1200" decoding="async" height="227" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/99/Amanita_phalloides_1.JPG/170px-Amanita_phalloides_1.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/99/Amanita_phalloides_1.JPG/255px-Amanita_phalloides_1.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/99/Amanita_phalloides_1.JPG/340px-Amanita_phalloides_1.JPG 2x" width="170"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Amanita_phalloides_1.JPG" title="放大"></a></div><a href="/wiki/%E6%AF%92%E9%B5%9D%E8%86%8F" title="毒鵝膏">毒鵝膏</a>造成了全世界超過一半<a href="/wiki/%E8%95%88%E9%A1%9E%E4%B8%AD%E6%AF%92" title="蕈類中毒">蕈類中毒</a>造成的死亡</div></div></div>
<p>許多真菌對人類是有毒的，毒性可輕至造成腸胃不適或過敏，重至產生幻覺、器官衰竭甚至致死。有毒的蕈類包括<a href="/wiki/%E9%94%A5%E7%9B%96%E4%BC%9E%E5%B1%9E" title="锥盖伞属">錐蓋傘屬</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E7%9B%94%E5%AD%A2%E4%BC%9E%E5%B1%9E" title="盔孢伞属">盔孢傘屬</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E7%8E%AF%E6%9F%84%E8%8F%87%E5%B1%9E" title="环柄菇属">環柄菇屬</a>與最惡名昭彰的<a href="/wiki/%E9%B5%9D%E8%86%8F%E8%8F%8C%E5%B1%AC" title="鵝膏菌屬">鵝膏菌屬</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Orr1979_237-0"><a href="#cite_note-Orr1979-237">[231]</a></sup>，鵝膏菌屬包含號稱毀滅天使的<a href="/wiki/%E9%B1%97%E6%9F%84%E7%99%BD%E9%B5%9D%E8%86%8F" title="鱗柄白鵝膏">鱗柄白鵝膏</a>與<a href="/wiki/%E6%AF%92%E9%B5%9D%E8%86%8F" title="毒鵝膏">毒鵝膏</a>，後者常被誤認成可食用的<a href="/wiki/%E8%8D%89%E8%8F%87" title="草菇">草菇</a>而誤食致死，佔人類因毒菇中毒死亡的比例超過半數<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Vetter1998_238-0"><a href="#cite_note-Vetter1998-238">[232]</a></sup> 。<a href="/wiki/%E9%B9%BF%E8%8A%B1%E8%8F%8C" title="鹿花菌">鹿花菌</a>煮熟後一般可以食用，且被許多人視為美食，但生食則有劇毒<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Leathem2007_239-0"><a href="#cite_note-Leathem2007-239">[233]</a></sup>，<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Tricholoma equestre" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="油口蘑"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%B2%B9%E5%8F%A3%E8%98%91&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="油口蘑（页面不存在）">油口蘑</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tricholoma_equestre" title="en:Tricholoma equestre"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Tricholoma equestre</span></a></span>）</span></span>甚至在<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%B8%AD%E4%B8%96%E7%B4%80" title="中世紀">中世紀</a>長期被認為可以食用，且受到某些<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%A8%8E%E5%A3%AB" title="騎士">騎士</a>的喜愛，後來才發現這種蕈類有劇毒，會導致<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%A9%AB%E7%B4%8B%E8%82%8C%E6%BA%B6%E8%A7%A3%E7%97%87" title="橫紋肌溶解症">橫紋肌溶解症</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-KarlsonStiber2003_240-0"><a href="#cite_note-KarlsonStiber2003-240">[234]</a></sup>。<a href="/wiki/%E6%AF%92%E8%A0%85%E5%82%98" title="毒蠅傘">毒蠅傘</a>也常造成不致死的中毒，多半是當<a href="/wiki/%E8%87%B4%E5%B9%BB%E5%89%82" title="致幻剂">致幻劑</a>吸食所造成，歷史上毒蠅傘曾被歐洲與亞洲的許多人群拿來吸食，直到現在仍被<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%A7%91%E9%87%8C%E4%BA%9E%E5%85%8B%E6%97%8F" title="科里亞克族">科里亞克族</a>等<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%A5%BF%E4%BC%AF%E5%88%A9%E4%BA%9E" title="西伯利亞">西伯利亞</a>東北部的民族在<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%96%A9%E6%BB%BF%E6%95%99" title="薩滿教">薩滿教</a>儀式上用做致幻性藥品<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Michelot2003_241-0"><a href="#cite_note-Michelot2003-241">[235]</a></sup>。
</p><p>未受專業訓練的人很難正確分辨蕈類是否可食，因此專家通常建議將所有在野外發現的蕈類視為有毒的，不要食用<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-242"><a href="#cite_note-242">[236]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Ammirati1987_243-0"><a href="#cite_note-Ammirati1987-243">[237]</a></sup>。若誤食毒菇出現症狀，應保留剩下的菇與嘔吐物等檢體並立即就醫<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-244"><a href="#cite_note-244">[238]</a></sup>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E8.9F.B2.E5.AE.B3.E7.AE.A1.E7.90.86"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="蟲害管理">蟲害管理</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%9C%9F%E8%8F%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;section=40" title="编辑章节：蟲害管理">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Beauveria.jpg"><img alt="Two dead grasshoppers with a whitish fuzz growing on them" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1166" data-file-width="1200" decoding="async" height="214" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c3/Beauveria.jpg/220px-Beauveria.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c3/Beauveria.jpg/330px-Beauveria.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c3/Beauveria.jpg/440px-Beauveria.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Beauveria.jpg" title="放大"></a></div>被<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Beauveria bassiana" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="巴氏蠶白僵菌"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%B7%B4%E6%B0%8F%E8%A0%B6%E7%99%BD%E5%83%B5%E8%8F%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="巴氏蠶白僵菌（页面不存在）">巴氏蠶白僵菌</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Beauveria_bassiana" title="en:Beauveria bassiana"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Beauveria bassiana</span></a></span>）</span></span>殺死的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%9A%B1%E8%9C%A2" title="蚱蜢">蚱蜢</a></div></div></div>
<p>在農業上，根據<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%AB%B6%E7%88%AD%E6%8E%92%E9%99%A4%E5%8E%9F%E5%89%87" title="競爭排除原則">競爭排除原則</a>，真菌若可以與有害的細菌或其他真菌競爭資源與空間，甚至寄生這些微生物，抑制有害菌，都可用作<a href="/wiki/%E7%94%9F%E7%89%A9%E9%98%B2%E6%B2%BB" title="生物防治">生物防治</a>以減少病蟲害<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-LopezGomez2006_245-0"><a href="#cite_note-LopezGomez2006-245">[239]</a></sup>。許多真菌可抑制<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%9F%8E" title="蟎">蟎</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E6%9D%82%E8%8D%89" title="杂草">雜草</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%BA%BF%E8%99%AB" title="线虫">線蟲</a>或其他有害於作物的真菌生長<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-urlUSDA_Biocontrol_246-0"><a href="#cite_note-urlUSDA_Biocontrol-246">[240]</a></sup>，在生物防治上產生了許多應用。<a href="/wiki/%E8%99%AB%E7%94%9F%E7%9C%9F%E8%8F%8C" title="虫生真菌">蟲生真菌</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-urlwww.uvminnovations.com_247-0"><a href="#cite_note-urlwww.uvminnovations.com-247">[241]</a></sup>如<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Beauveria bassiana" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="白殭菌"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%99%BD%E5%83%B5%E8%8F%8C" title="白僵菌">白殭菌</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Beauveria_bassiana" title="en:Beauveria bassiana"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Beauveria bassiana</span></a></span>）</span></span>、<a href="/wiki/%E9%BB%91%E6%AE%AD%E8%8F%8C" title="黑殭菌">黑殭菌</a>、<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Hirsutella" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="被毛孢"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%A2%AB%E6%AF%9B%E5%AD%A2&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="被毛孢（页面不存在）">被毛孢</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hirsutella" title="en:Hirsutella"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Hirsutella</span></a></span>）</span></span>、<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Paecilomyces" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="擬青黴菌"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%93%AC%E9%9D%92%E9%BB%B4%E8%8F%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="擬青黴菌（页面不存在）">擬青黴菌</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Paecilomyces" title="en:Paecilomyces"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Paecilomyces</span></a></span>）</span></span>與<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Lecanicillium lecanii" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="蠟蚧輪枝菌"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%A0%9F%E8%9A%A7%E8%BC%AA%E6%9E%9D%E8%8F%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="蠟蚧輪枝菌（页面不存在）">蠟蚧輪枝菌</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lecanicillium_lecanii" title="en:Lecanicillium lecanii"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Lecanicillium lecanii</span></a></span>）</span></span>等皆可抑制害蟲生長而用作<a href="/wiki/%E7%94%9F%E7%89%A9%E8%BE%B2%E8%97%A5" title="生物農藥">生物農藥</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Deshpande1999_248-0"><a href="#cite_note-Deshpande1999-248">[242]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Thomas2007_249-0"><a href="#cite_note-Thomas2007-249">[243]</a></sup>。<i>Neotyphodium</i>、<a href="/wiki/%E9%A6%99%E6%9F%B1%E8%8F%8C%E5%B1%9E" title="香柱菌属">香柱菌屬</a>等內生真菌生長在植物體內，可以合成<a href="/wiki/%E7%94%9F%E7%89%A9%E9%B9%BC" title="生物鹼">生物鹼</a>以避免植物受到<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%8D%89%E9%A3%9F%E5%8B%95%E7%89%A9" title="草食動物">草食動物</a>啃食<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Bush1997_250-0"><a href="#cite_note-Bush1997-250">[244]</a></sup>，這種特性也被人利用在<a href="/wiki/%E6%94%BE%E7%89%A7%E5%A0%B4" title="放牧場">放牧場</a>等草地的栽培中，經由<a href="/wiki/%E6%A4%8D%E7%89%A9%E9%85%8D%E7%A8%AE" title="植物配種">植物配種</a>選擇分泌物只對昆蟲有毒性，而對家畜無害真菌<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Bouton2002_251-0"><a href="#cite_note-Bouton2002-251">[245]</a></sup>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E7.9C.9F.E8.8F.8C.E4.BF.AE.E5.BE.A9"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="真菌修復">真菌修復</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%9C%9F%E8%8F%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;section=41" title="编辑章节：真菌修復">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a href="/wiki/%E7%9C%9F%E8%8F%8C%E4%BF%AE%E5%BE%A9" title="真菌修復">真菌修復</a></div>
<p>真菌修復是<a href="/wiki/%E7%94%9F%E7%89%A9%E4%BF%AE%E5%BE%A9" title="生物修復">生物修復</a>的一種，意指以真菌來降解環境中的汙染物。已知某些真菌可以將<a href="/wiki/%E6%AE%BA%E8%9F%B2%E5%8A%91" title="殺蟲劑">殺蟲劑</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%99%A4%E8%8D%89%E5%8A%91" title="除草劑">除草劑</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%B6%88%E6%AF%92%E5%8A%91" title="消毒劑">消毒劑</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E7%9F%BF%E7%89%A9%E6%9D%82%E9%85%9A%E6%B2%B9" title="矿物杂酚油">礦物雜酚油</a>、甚至長鏈石油分解成二氧化碳與水<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Christian2005_252-0"><a href="#cite_note-Christian2005-252">[246]</a></sup>，還可以吸收環境中的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%87%8D%E9%87%91%E5%B1%AC" title="重金屬">重金屬</a>並儲存於子實體中。有些真菌甚至能用來清理受<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%A0%B8%E6%B1%A1%E6%9F%93" title="核污染">核污染</a>的土地，<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-BBC2008_253-0"><a href="#cite_note-BBC2008-253">[247]</a></sup>核廢料中的<a href="/wiki/%E8%B2%A7%E9%88%BE" title="貧鈾">貧鈾</a>在環境中容易被氧化，而鈾氧化物可以被植物與細菌所吸收，在食物鏈中層層累積。真菌可以經由<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Biomineralization" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="生物礦化作用"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%94%9F%E7%89%A9%E7%A4%A6%E5%8C%96%E4%BD%9C%E7%94%A8&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="生物礦化作用（页面不存在）">生物礦化作用</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Biomineralization" title="en:Biomineralization"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Biomineralization</span></a></span>）</span></span>將鈾氧化物固定成磷酸鹽礦物，這種型式的鈾不易被生物所吸收，不會進入食物鏈中對生物造成危害<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Fomina2007_254-0"><a href="#cite_note-Fomina2007-254">[248]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Fomina2008_255-0"><a href="#cite_note-Fomina2008-255">[249]</a></sup>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E6.A8.A1.E5.BC.8F.E7.94.9F.E7.89.A9"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="模式生物">模式生物</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%9C%9F%E8%8F%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;section=42" title="编辑章节：模式生物">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>許多生物學上的重大發現都得益於將真菌用作<a href="/wiki/%E6%A8%A1%E5%BC%8F%E7%94%9F%E7%89%A9" title="模式生物">模式生物</a>的研究，例如<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="One gene–one enzyme hypothesis" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="一基因一酵素假說"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%B8%80%E5%9F%BA%E5%9B%A0%E4%B8%80%E9%85%B5%E7%B4%A0%E5%81%87%E8%AA%AA&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="一基因一酵素假說（页面不存在）">一基因一酵素假說</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/One_gene%E2%80%93one_enzyme_hypothesis" title="en:One gene–one enzyme hypothesis"><span dir="auto" lang="en">One gene–one enzyme hypothesis</span></a></span>）</span></span>便是用<a href="/wiki/%E7%B2%89%E8%89%B2%E9%BA%B5%E5%8C%85%E9%BB%B4%E8%8F%8C" title="粉色麵包黴菌">粉色麵包黴菌</a>的實驗證實的<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Beadle1941_256-0"><a href="#cite_note-Beadle1941-256">[250]</a></sup>。<a href="/wiki/%E9%87%80%E9%85%92%E9%85%B5%E6%AF%8D" title="釀酒酵母">釀酒酵母</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%A3%82%E6%AE%96%E9%85%B5%E6%AF%8D" title="裂殖酵母">裂殖酵母</a>與<a href="/wiki/%E5%B0%8F%E5%B7%A2%E7%8B%80%E9%BA%B4%E8%8F%8C" title="小巢狀麴菌">小巢狀麴菌</a>也都是重要的模式生物，長久以來用於有關<a href="/wiki/%E7%B4%B0%E8%83%9E%E9%80%B1%E6%9C%9F" title="細胞週期">細胞週期</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%9F%93%E8%89%B2%E9%AB%94" title="染色體">染色體</a>結構與<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Regulation of gene expression" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="基因表現調控"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9F%BA%E5%9B%A0%E8%A1%A8%E7%8F%BE%E8%AA%BF%E6%8E%A7&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="基因表現調控（页面不存在）">基因表現調控</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Regulation_of_gene_expression" title="en:Regulation of gene expression"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Regulation of gene expression</span></a></span>）</span></span>等<a href="/wiki/%E7%9C%9F%E6%A0%B8%E7%94%9F%E7%89%A9" title="真核生物">真核生物</a><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%81%BA%E5%82%B3%E5%AD%B8" title="遺傳學">遺傳學</a>與<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%B4%B0%E8%83%9E%E7%94%9F%E7%89%A9%E5%AD%B8" title="細胞生物學">細胞生物學</a>的基礎研究。近年來有更多真菌被當成醫學、植物病理與工業研究的模式生物，例如人類的病原菌<a href="/wiki/%E7%99%BD%E8%89%B2%E5%BF%B5%E7%8F%A0%E8%8F%8C" title="白色念珠菌">白色念珠菌</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Datta1989_257-0"><a href="#cite_note-Datta1989-257">[251]</a></sup>、植物病原菌<a href="/wiki/%E7%A8%BB%E7%86%B1%E7%97%85%E8%8F%8C" title="稻熱病菌">稻熱病菌</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Dean2005_258-0"><a href="#cite_note-Dean2005-258">[252]</a></sup>與工業上常用來大量生產真核生物蛋白質的<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Pichia pastoris" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="嗜甲醇酵母菌"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%97%9C%E7%94%B2%E9%86%87%E9%85%B5%E6%AF%8D%E8%8F%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="嗜甲醇酵母菌（页面不存在）">嗜甲醇酵母菌</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pichia_pastoris" title="en:Pichia pastoris"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Pichia pastoris</span></a></span>）</span></span><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Daly2005_259-0"><a href="#cite_note-Daly2005-259">[253]</a></sup>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E5.85.B6.E4.BB.96"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="其他">其他</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%9C%9F%E8%8F%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;section=43" title="编辑章节：其他">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>真菌被廣泛用來生產<a href="/wiki/%E6%AA%B8%E6%AA%AC%E9%85%B8" title="檸檬酸">檸檬酸</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E8%91%A1%E8%90%84%E7%B3%96%E9%85%B8" title="葡萄糖酸">葡萄糖酸</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E4%B9%B3%E9%85%B8" title="乳酸">乳酸</a>與<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%98%8B%E6%9E%9C%E9%85%B8" title="蘋果酸">蘋果酸</a>等化學物質<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Schlegel1993_260-0"><a href="#cite_note-Schlegel1993-260">[254]</a></sup> ，以及工業用的酵素，例如<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%B4%97%E8%A1%A3%E7%B2%89" title="洗衣粉">洗衣粉</a>裡的<a href="/wiki/%E8%84%82%E9%85%B6" title="脂酶">脂酶</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Joseph2008_261-0"><a href="#cite_note-Joseph2008-261">[255]</a></sup>、用來生產<a href="/wiki/%E7%BA%96%E7%B6%AD%E7%B4%A0%E4%B9%99%E9%86%87" title="纖維素乙醇">纖維素乙醇</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Kumar2008_262-0"><a href="#cite_note-Kumar2008-262">[256]</a></sup>和<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%89%9B%E4%BB%94%E8%A4%B2" title="牛仔褲">牛仔褲</a><span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Stone washing" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="酵素石洗"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%85%B5%E7%B4%A0%E7%9F%B3%E6%B4%97&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="酵素石洗（页面不存在）">酵素石洗</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Stone_washing" title="en:Stone washing"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Stone washing</span></a></span>）</span></span><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-nysaes_263-0"><a href="#cite_note-nysaes-263">[257]</a></sup>的<a href="/wiki/%E7%BA%A4%E7%BB%B4%E7%B4%A0%E9%85%B6" title="纤维素酶">纖維素酶</a>、以及<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%BE%B1%E7%B2%89%E9%85%B6" title="澱粉酶">澱粉酶</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-OlempskaBeer2006_264-0"><a href="#cite_note-OlempskaBeer2006-264">[258]</a></sup>、<a href="/wiki/%E8%94%97%E7%B3%96%E9%85%B6" title="蔗糖酶">蔗糖酶</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E8%9B%8B%E7%99%BD%E9%85%B6" title="蛋白酶">蛋白酶</a>與<a href="/wiki/%E6%9C%A8%E8%81%9A%E7%B3%96%E9%85%B6" title="木聚糖酶">木聚糖酶</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Polizeli2005_265-0"><a href="#cite_note-Polizeli2005-265">[259]</a></sup>。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E5.8F.83.E8.A6.8B"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="參見">參見</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%9C%9F%E8%8F%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;section=44" title="编辑章节：參見">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div aria-label="Portals" class="noprint portal plainlist tright" role="navigation" style="margin:0.5em 0 0.5em 1em;border:solid #aaa 1px">
<ul style="display:table;box-sizing:border-box;padding:0.1em;max-width:175px;background:#f9f9f9;font-size:85%;line-height:110%;font-weight:bold">
<li style="display:table-row"><span style="display:table-cell;padding:0.2em;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center"><img alt="" class="noviewer" data-file-height="1215" data-file-width="1105" decoding="async" height="28" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/42/Karl_Johanssvamp%2C_Iduns_kokbok.png/25px-Karl_Johanssvamp%2C_Iduns_kokbok.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/42/Karl_Johanssvamp%2C_Iduns_kokbok.png/38px-Karl_Johanssvamp%2C_Iduns_kokbok.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/42/Karl_Johanssvamp%2C_Iduns_kokbok.png/51px-Karl_Johanssvamp%2C_Iduns_kokbok.png 2x" width="25"/></span><span style="display:table-cell;padding:0.2em 0.2em 0.2em 0.3em;vertical-align:middle"><a href="/wiki/Portal:%E7%9C%9F%E8%8F%8C" title="Portal:真菌">真菌主题</a></span></li></ul></div>

<h2><span id=".E8.A8.BB.E8.85.B3"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="註腳">註腳</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%9C%9F%E8%8F%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;section=45" title="编辑章节：註腳">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div id="references-NoteFoot"><ol class="references">
<li id="cite_note-79"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-79">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">為舊時分類，因爲是<a href="/wiki/%E4%B8%A6%E7%B3%BB%E7%BE%A4" title="並系群">並系群</a>，現已被分拆成多個不同的門。詳見<a href="#分類">#分類</a>一節</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-108"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-108">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">也是舊分類名詞，現在已不使用，約等同於現在的<a href="/wiki/%E5%82%98%E8%8F%8C%E7%B6%B1" title="傘菌綱">傘菌綱</a></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-121"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-121">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">部分中文翻譯參考 <cite class="citation book">贺新生. <a class="external text" href="http://www.ecsponline.com/goods.php?id=169066" rel="nofollow">现代菌物分类系统</a>. <a href="/wiki/%E7%A7%91%E5%AD%A6%E5%87%BA%E7%89%88%E7%A4%BE" title="科学出版社">科學出版社</a>. 2015 <span class="reference-accessdate"> [<span class="nowrap">2018-07-18</span>]</span>. <a href="/wiki/Special:%E7%BD%91%E7%BB%9C%E4%B9%A6%E6%BA%90/9787030451637" title="Special:网络书源/9787030451637"><span title="国际标准书号">ISBN</span> 9787030451637</a>. （原始内容<a class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20210115134207/http://www.ecsponline.com/goods.php?id=169066" rel="nofollow">存档</a>于2021-01-15）.</cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E7%9C%9F%E8%8F%8C&amp;rft.au=%E8%B4%BA%E6%96%B0%E7%94%9F&amp;rft.btitle=%E7%8E%B0%E4%BB%A3%E8%8F%8C%E7%89%A9%E5%88%86%E7%B1%BB%E7%B3%BB%E7%BB%9F&amp;rft.date=2015&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.isbn=9787030451637&amp;rft.pub=%E7%A7%91%E5%AD%B8%E5%87%BA%E7%89%88%E7%A4%BE&amp;rft_id=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.ecsponline.com%2Fgoods.php%3Fid%3D169066&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-122"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-122">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">此為傳統分類中屬於Eumycota的類群</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-124"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-124">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%A0%B8%E5%BD%A2%E8%9F%B2" title="核形蟲">核形蟲</a>與<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Fonticula" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="泉生蟲"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%B3%89%E7%94%9F%E8%9F%B2&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="泉生蟲（页面不存在）">泉生蟲</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fonticula" title="en:Fonticula"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Fonticula</span></a></span>）</span></span>都沒有<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%B9%BE%E4%B8%81%E8%B3%AA" title="幾丁質">幾丁質</a>組成的<a href="/wiki/%E7%B4%B0%E8%83%9E%E5%A3%81" title="細胞壁">細胞壁</a>，具有圓盤狀的粒線體皺褶，以<a href="/wiki/%E8%AE%8A%E5%BD%A2%E8%9F%B2" title="變形蟲">變形蟲</a>的型態生長，以<a href="/wiki/%E5%90%9E%E5%99%AC%E4%BD%9C%E7%94%A8" title="吞噬作用">吞噬作用</a>取得養分，<a href="/wiki/%E5%9F%BA%E5%9B%A0%E7%B5%84" title="基因組">基因組</a>中缺少第二型（Division II）<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="chitin synthetase" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="幾丁質合成酶"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%B9%BE%E4%B8%81%E8%B3%AA%E5%90%88%E6%88%90%E9%85%B6&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="幾丁質合成酶（页面不存在）">幾丁質合成酶</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/chitin_synthetase" title="en:chitin synthetase"><span dir="auto" lang="en">chitin synthetase</span></a></span>）</span></span>的基因，這些特徵都與真菌不同。隱真菌門雖然也有許多物種缺乏細胞壁，但它們仍有第二型幾丁質合成酶的基因，細胞壁的缺乏可能是該演化支分支以後才丟失的特徵<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Tedersoo2018_2-4"><a href="#cite_note-Tedersoo2018-2">[2]</a></sup></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-125"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-125">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">這四個亞門隨後在不同研究中，分別被提升至門的地位</span>
</li>
</ol></div>
<h2><span id=".E5.8F.82.E8.80.83.E6.96.87.E7.8C.AE"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="参考文献">参考文献</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%9C%9F%E8%8F%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;section=46" title="编辑章节：参考文献">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
